ptolomeus philopater kinge egipt yere worlde yere christe reygned xvii yeres slue parentes brother inuaded theyr royalme philip king macedon gouerned yeres warres social betwene acheans aetolians annybal sonne amilcar ordeined capitain carthage like noble valyaunte courage wise gilefull wonderfull polycy wherby wrought much scath roman conceiued enmitee wrath youth beynge childe viii yeares
